# command

```
sudo ./docker-ubuntu.sh 
sudo docker run -it -p 1880:1880 testing:node-red-build-ubuntu
sudo docker run -it -p 1880:1880 -v node_red_data:/data testing:node-red-build-ubuntu
sudo docker run -it -p 1880:1880 -v node_red_data:/data --name mynodered-6 testing:node-red-build-ubuntu
sudo docker run -it -p 1880:1880 --network=host -v node_red_data:/data --name mynodered-6 testing:node-red-build-ubuntu
```
